DICOM images from the local drive, removable media or PACS servers like you’ve never done before.\r\n\r\nThe all new Navegatium 3D Printing module, the innovative on demand 3D printing service allows you to request 3D printed biomodels from exams directly on the app.\r\n\r\n► Import from local media, PACS or the cloud\r\n\r\nQuickly find and organize your DICOM studies.
